<p><em>2) Transition of HRD testing to NGS is significantly influenced by the price per sample. There are no reimbursements in place, hospitals must fund the HRD test from their existing budget (which is tailored to TSO500 excl. HRD)</em></p>

<p><em></em></p>

<p><em>3) Following discussions with the customers at the 2 user group meetings during Q4 2023, we concluded that 270EUR per sample is the highest acceptable additional cost for the hospitals. This insight was gathered from both the Oncology Specialist and TAMs.</em></p>

<p><em></em></p>

<p><em>4) The proposed price will accelerate and guarantee implementation and equal access to HRD testing across all the Pathology Centres in The Netherlands.</em></p>

<p><em></em></p>

<p><em>5) Being the first player and district to implement HRD at a national/high- level will strengthen the competitive positioning of TSO500/HRD locally and on European level</em></p>
